	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

		name = USA.3.a
	}

news_event = {
	id = USA.24
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.24" }
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			70 = { USA = { country_event = { id = USA.25 } } }
			30 = { USA = { country_event = { id = USA.26 } } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.24.a
	}
}

#Mccormack decides whether or not he wants to try and pull the RDs together
country_event = {
	#id = USA.33
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.33" }
	title = USA.33.t
	desc = USA.33.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_rdc_generic_1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #we must try
		name = USA.33.a
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_to_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_mccormack_against_npp }
		USA_reload_nixon_tree = yes
	}
	option = { #it's not my place
		name = USA.33.b
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

country_event = { #South African ambassador meets with the Americans, assured that this time they actually have shit to say. For once they don't press on joining the OFN, and get down to buisness in terms of ensuring SAF's protection
	id = USA.ct.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.ct.2" }
	title = USA.ct.2.t
	desc = USA.ct.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MZB_quelimane

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Awesome!
		name = USA.ct.2.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SAF
			modifier = USA_South_africa_Working_Together
		}
		SAF = {
			add_stability = 0.02
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_South_africa_Working_Together }
		}
	}
}

######################################################################33
country_event = {#Form the CAR?
	id = USA.51
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.51" }
	title = USA.51.t
	desc = USA.51.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress_4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Form the CAR
		name = USA.51.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAR_FATE_PATH option = CAR_FATE_PATH_NO }
			}
			modifier = {
				SAF = {
					NOT = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = OFN_AFR_MANDATE.1 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { #Keep the three administrations
		name = USA.51.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAR_FATE_PATH option = CAR_FATE_PATH_YES }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#country_event = { id = USA.saf.effects.18 days = 3 } #missing event for start of insurgencies in Africa, duplicate event slot with total SAW vic
			country_event = { id = OFN_AFR_MANDATE.0 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Protests against conscription for the SAF War
country_event = {
	id = USA.55
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.55" }
	title = USA.55.t
	desc = USA.55.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_luke_on_tatooine

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.55.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = USA_conscription_riot } }
			add_ideas = USA_conscription_riot
		}
 		#hidden_effect = {
 		#	country_event = { id = USA.53 days = 8 }
 		#}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_npp_5_increase
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = US_election_state }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#US invites SAF to the OFN
country_event = {
	id = USA.61
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.61" }
	title = USA.61.t
	desc = USA.61.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_pentagon_1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.61.a
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = SAF
				add_to_array = { OFN_members = SAF }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.61.b
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = USA.67
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.67" }
	title = USA.67.t
	desc = USA.67.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_USA_jfk_and_mlk
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.67.a
		trigger = { tag = USA }
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.67.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.67.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.67.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = USA }
			is_in_faction_with = USA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.67.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = USA
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Civil Rights Act - veto
news_event = {
	id = USA.68
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.68" }
	title = USA.68.t
	desc = USA.68.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_USA_veto_cra
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.68.a
		trigger = { tag = USA }
		set_country_flag = USA_flag_nixon_CRA_vetoed
		custom_effect_tooltip = NPP_shift_left
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_nixon_cra_veto
		add_ideas = USA_North_Discontent_1
		set_variable = { USA_North_Discontent_ticker = 0 }
		set_variable = { USA_North_Discontent_change = 1 }

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_voters_header_tt
		set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_pro = 4 }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_pro }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_urban_pro_shift
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_urban_pro_val = .03 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_black_voters_header_tt
		set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_black_pro = 8 }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_pro }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_black_pro_shift
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_black_pro_val = .04 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_hispanic_voters_header_tt
		set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_hispanic_pro = 8 }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_hispanic_pro }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_hispanic_pro_shift
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_hispanic_pro_val = .04 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_nativists_voters_header_tt #dixiecrats
		set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_nativists_rep = 8 }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_nativists_rep }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_nativists_rep_shift
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_nativists_rep_val = .02 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rural_voters_header_tt
		set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_rural_rep = 5 }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_rep }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rural_rep_shift
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_rural_rep_val = .03 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

		USA_add_15_DC_RDC_approval = yes
		USA_add_5_HR_RDC_approval = yes

		USA_remove_10_LD_RDC_approval = yes
		USA_remove_10_RR_RDC_approval = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			USA_all_demographic_shifts = yes
		}

		US_election_update_gui_post_senate = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.68.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.68.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.68.d
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = USA
			NOT = { tag = USA }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.68.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = USA
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Pro-civil rights demonstration
country_event = {
	id = USA.71
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.71" }
	title = USA.71.t
	desc = USA.71.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_rights_2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.71.a
		set_country_flag = USA_pro_civil_rights_demonstrations
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA.72 days = 3 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_all_voters_header_tt
		set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_black_civil_rights_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib }
		add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_hispanic_civil_rights_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib }
		add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_minority_civil_rights_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib }
		add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_nativists_civil_rights_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib }
		add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_urban_civil_rights_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib }
		add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_rural_civil_rights_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib }
		add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_union_civil_rights_lib_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_civil_rights_lib }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_black_civil_rights_lib
	}
}

			}

			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_nixon_impeached_b4

			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_pro = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_nat = 8 }
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NIXON_RESIG_SAVE_FACE_TT
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_pro = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_nat = 5 }
		}	

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_all_voters_header_tt
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_pro_shift
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_urban_pro_val = .02 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_union_pro_val = .025 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_rural_pro_val = .005 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_black_pro_val = .02 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_hispanic_pro_val = .02 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_minority_pro_val = .01 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_nativists_pro_val = .005 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_nat_shift
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
		add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_urban_nat_val = .01 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_union_nat_val = .02 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_rural_nat_val = .02 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_nativists_nat_val = .025 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_bonus_tooltip

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { bill_id = 103 } }

			set_variable = { USA_prev_president = USA_president }

			US_elections_calculate_country_vars = yes
			remove_ideas = USA_John_F_Kennedy_hog
			add_ideas = USA_John_McCormack_hog
			promote_character = USA_John_F_Kennedy
			promote_character = USA_Wallace_F_Bennett

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = liberalism
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			add_to_variable = { US_presidents = 1 }
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_unity = 1 }
			US_elections_calculate_country_vars = yes

		}

country_event = {
	id = USA.130
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.130 NPP primary" }
	title = USA.130.t
	desc = { text = USA.130.desc_cr_passed
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_civil_rights_passed }
	}
	desc = { text = USA.130.desc_cr_blocked
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_civil_rights_blocked }
	}
	desc = { text = USA.130.desc_cr_neutral
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_nixon_neutral }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_npp_generic_1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.130.a #George Wallace
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_civil_rights_blocked }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_wallace_primary_64
		set_variable = { USA.NPP_civil_rights_policy = 2 }
		set_variable = { USA.NPP_domestic_policy_policy = 2 }
		set_variable = { USA.NPP_economic_policy_policy = 3 }
		set_variable = { USA.NPP_foreign_policy_policy = 5 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_johnson_nominated
			}
			#set_variable = { USA.RDC_civil_rights_policy = 9 } #mango if you see this I commented this out to see if this helps with Wallace sweeping
			#set_variable = { USA.RDC_domestic_policy_policy = 9 }
			#set_variable = { USA.RDC_economic_policy_policy = 3 }
			#set_variable = { USA.RDC_foreign_policy_policy = 9 }


			set_variable = { USA.NPP_civil_rights_policy = 3 }
			set_variable = { USA.NPP_domestic_policy_policy = 3 }
			set_variable = { USA.NPP_economic_policy_policy = 5 }
			set_variable = { USA.NPP_foreign_policy_policy = 5 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_nationalist_running
			set_country_flag = nat_can_pres
			set_country_flag = USA_wallace_nominated
			set_variable = { USA_current_election_npp_candidate = 7 }
			set_country_flag = npp_primary_done
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = npp_primary_done
					has_country_flag = rdc_primary_done
				}
				USA_debate_64_effect = yes
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 NPP primaries: Wallace"
			country_event = { id = USA.early_flavor.9 days = 32 }
			USA_GUI_check_to_update_screen = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.130.b #RFK
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_civil_rights_passed }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_RFK_primary_64
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_progressive_running set_country_flag = pro_can_pres
			set_country_flag = USA_kennedy_nominated
			set_variable = { USA.NPP_civil_rights_policy = 7 }
			set_variable = { USA.NPP_domestic_policy_policy = 7 }
			set_variable = { USA.NPP_economic_policy_policy = 6 }
			set_variable = { USA.NPP_foreign_policy_policy = 9 }


			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_johnson_nominated
						has_country_flag = USA_hart_nominated
					}
				}
				set_variable = { USA.RDC_civil_rights_policy = 2 }
				set_variable = { USA.RDC_domestic_policy_policy = 3 }
				set_variable = { USA.RDC_economic_policy_policy = 3 }
				set_variable = { USA.RDC_foreign_policy_policy = 4 }
			}

			set_variable = { USA_current_election_npp_candidate = 8 }
			set_country_flag = npp_primary_done
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = npp_primary_done
					has_country_flag = rdc_primary_done
				}
				USA_debate_64_effect = yes
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 RD primaries: Kennedy"
			USA_GUI_check_to_update_screen = yes
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = USA.135
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.135" }
	title = USA.135.t
	desc = USA.135.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_capitol_building_2

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_presidential_election_conclusion = yes
			clr_country_flag = currently_campaigning
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = USA_debug_quadweekly_printing has_country_flag = USA_debug_printing_all } }
				USA_print_pop_to_log = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.12 days = 30 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.136 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Bennett"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.137 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Johnson"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.138 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Wallace"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.139 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Kennedy"
			}
			set_variable = { US_debt_expectation = debt_to_GDP_ratio }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Wallace F. Bennett
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 } }
		name = USA.135.a
	}
	option = { #LBJ
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 } }
		name = USA.135.b
	}
	option = { #George Wallace
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 } }
		name = USA.135.c
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = wallace.629 days = 13 } }
	}
	option = { #RFK
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 } }
		name = USA.135.d
	}
}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			set_variable = { USA_prev_president = USA_president }
			set_variable = { USA_president = GOLDWATER }
			clr_country_flag = USA_show_NPP_screen

			promote_character = USA_Barry_Goldwater
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.711
					days = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { USA_CIA_Lead = token:Espionage_Bissell }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_NA } check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_CA } check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_SA } } }
				set_variable = { TNO_Espionage_AgencyLeader = USA_CIA_Lead }
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter min = 0 }
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_68_R_RDC
			set_country_flag = USA_68_R_RDC_Past
			377 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_R_name = 1 } } # Goldwater no longer uses the seat
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = conservatism
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Walter_Judd_hog
			add_ideas = USA_Carl_Curtis_for
			add_ideas = USA_Donald_Regan_eco
			add_ideas = USA_Robert_McNamara_sec_gold
			384 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_RD_D_name = 1 } } # Curtis abandons his seat
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_68_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_GLD_68
			if = { #Check if the response mission should activate
				limit = { #Either LBJ, RFK or Wallace was president
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP_Past
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_begin_response
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = USA.neo_silver.1 days = 117 } }
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.161.a
		USA_fire_succession_event_Goldwater = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = USA_schlafly_flavor.18
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}

# 163 - Michael Harrington
country_event = { #Harrington Inauguration
	id = USA.163
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.163" }
	title = USA.163.t
	desc = USA.163.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_people

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			set_variable = { USA_prev_president = USA_president }
			set_variable = { USA_president = HARRINGTON }
			set_country_flag = USA_show_NPP_screen

			promote_character = USA_Michael_Harrington
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.713
					days = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { USA_CIA_Lead = token:Espionage_Jackson }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_NA } check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_CA } check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_SA } } }
				set_variable = { TNO_Espionage_AgencyLeader = USA_CIA_Lead }
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter min = 0 }
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
			set_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP_Past
			373 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = progressivism
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Irving_Howe_hog
			add_ideas = USA_Generic_Vacant_for
			add_ideas = USA_Generic_Vacant_eco
			add_ideas = USA_Generic_Vacant_sec
			387 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
			370 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_68_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_HAR_68
			if = { #Check if the response mission should activate
				limit = { #Either Bennett or Wallace was elected
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP_Past
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_begin_response
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC_Past }
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_LBJ_great_society_modifier }
			}
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_fatigue = 0 }

			set_variable = { USA_HAR_enthusiasm = 0 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_rich_enthusiasm = 45 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_middle_enthusiasm = 60 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poor_enthusiasm = 75 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poverty_enthusiasm = 90 }

			set_variable = { USA_HAR_rich_influence = 80 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_middle_influence = 60 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poor_influence = 35 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poverty_influence = 1 }

			#Give an enthusiaism bonus based on Harringtons electoral win margin
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_rich_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_middle_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_poor_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_poverty_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }

			#Put in place some reasonable limits on middle and upper classess so Harrington doesn't start with 100% approval
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_HAR_rich_enthusiasm max = 75 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_HAR_middle_enthusiasm max = 90 }

			clear_variable = USA_HAR_win_margin #No need for this anymore

			USA_HAR_calculate_enthusiasm = yes


			set_variable = { USA_HAR_fatigue_event_count = 0 }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = USA.neo_silver.1 days = 117 } }
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 4 }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = progressivism
				long_name = USA_S_NPP_Harrington_Presidency
				name = USA_S_NPP_Harrington_Presidency_short
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.163.a
		USA_fire_succession_event_Harrington = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = USA_schlafly_flavor.16
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = USA.174.t
	desc = USA.174.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_navy_hawaii

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Crush the Bund
		name = USA.174.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_alcatraz_crush
			random_list = {
				30 = { country_event = { id = USA.175 days = 4 } }
				70 = { country_event = { id = USA.176 days = 4 } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #The prisons are safe
		name = USA.174.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_alcatraz_safe
			random_list = {
				25 = { country_event = { id = USA.175 days = 4 } }
				75 = { country_event = { id = USA.176 days = 4 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Romney Inauguration
	id = USA.1701
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1701" }
	title = USA.1701.t
	desc = USA.1701.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_romney_button

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			set_variable = { USA_prev_president = USA_president }
			set_variable = { USA_president = ROMNEY }
			clr_country_flag = USA_show_NPP_screen

			set_variable = { USA_CIA_Lead = token:Espionage_Bush }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_NA } check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_CA } check_variable = { Region_v = token:Espionage_Map_SA } } }
				set_variable = { TNO_Espionage_AgencyLeader = USA_CIA_Lead }
			}
			promote_character = USA_George_Romney
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.721
					days = 1
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_72_R_RDC
			set_country_flag = USA_72_R_RDC_Past
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = conservatism
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			fill_empty_minister_nochecks = yes 

			set_country_flag = USA_mil_64_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_Romney_72
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.1701.a
		USA_fire_succession_event_Romney = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Checks if Jim Crow is still around in the 70s
	id = USA.1803
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1803" }
	title = USA.1803.t
	desc = USA.1803.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_pentagon_1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_idea = USA_jim_crow
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.1803.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_unity = 2 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_unity = 1 }
		}
	}
}

	title = USA.1917.t
	desc = USA.1917.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_cia_button

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.1917.a
		TNO_fopo_remove_IBW_tab = yes
		set_temp_variable = { target = SPR }
		TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { SPR = { exists = yes } }
			SPR = { econ_join_sphere_USA = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					SPS = { exists = yes }
					FZL = { exists = yes }
					SPR = { exists = yes }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { conclusion_weeks = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { conclusion_bonus = 0.02 }
			USA_proxy_conclusion_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { conclusion_weeks = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { conclusion_bonus = 0.01 }
			USA_proxy_conclusion_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = USA_elec_prim.1 #RD Primary 1968
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = USA_debug_quadweekly_printing has_country_flag = USA_debug_printing_all } }
				USA_print_pop_to_log = yes
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_elec_prim.1"
	}
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			has_government = progressivism
			has_government = paternalism
		}
	}
	title = USA_elec_prim.1.t
	desc = {
		text = USA_elec_prim.1_RD_Incumb
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC
				has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = USA_elec_prim.1_NPP_Incumb
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_LEMAY
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Barry Goldwater
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC
					has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC
				}
			}
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_RDC_PRIMARIES_1968 option = USA_RDC_PRIMARIES_1968_HART }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_republican_running set_country_flag = rep_can_pres
		set_country_flag = USA_goldwater_nominated
		set_variable = { USA.RDC_civil_rights_policy = 4 }
		set_variable = { USA.RDC_domestic_policy_policy = 3 }
		set_variable = { USA.RDC_economic_policy_policy = 3 }
		set_variable = { USA.RDC_foreign_policy_policy = 7 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 RD primaries: Goldwater"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			}
			set_variable = { USA_current_election_rd_candidate = 9 }
			set_country_flag = rdc_primary_done
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = npp_primary_done
					has_country_flag = rdc_primary_done
				}
				USA_debate_68_effect = yes
			}
			USA_GUI_check_to_update_screen = yes

	}

country_event = {
	id = USA_elec_prim.5 #US Election 1968
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_elec_prim.5" }
	title = USA_elec_prim.5.t
	desc = USA_elec_prim.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_busy_street
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_presidential_election_conclusion = yes
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = USA_debug_quadweekly_printing has_country_flag = USA_debug_printing_all } }
				USA_print_pop_to_log = yes
			}
			add_to_variable = { US_presidents = 1 }
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.12 days = 30 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.161 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Goldwater"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC }
				}
				country_event = { id = hart.1 days = 75 }
				country_event = { id = hart.misc.10 days = 8 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Hart"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.160 days = 75 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.17 days = 65 } #10 days before inauguration, MCS bennett meeting
				}
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Smith"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP }
				}

				set_variable = { USA_HAR_win_margin = US_current_total_pres_votes_npp }
				divide_variable = { USA_HAR_win_margin = 269 }
				country_event = { id = USA.163 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Harrington"
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC #LBJ 1 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.19 days = 35 } #LBJ Harry transition
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1731 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Bennett"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1732 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Johnson"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1734 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Wallace"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1733 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Kennedy"
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { #Barry Goldwater
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.5.a
	}
	option = { #Philip Hart
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.5.b
	}
	option = { #Margaret Chase Smith
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.5.c
	}
	option = { #Michael Harrington
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.5.d
	}
	option = { #Wallace F. Bennett reelection

			USA_presidential_election_conclusion = yes
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = USA_debug_quadweekly_printing has_country_flag = USA_debug_printing_all } }
				USA_print_pop_to_log = yes
			}
			add_to_variable = { US_presidents = 1 }
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.12 days = 30 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RDC }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1701 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Romney"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RDC }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1702 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Kirkpatrick"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1704 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Schlafly"
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC #Bennett 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.18 days = 15 } #Bennett-NPP transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC #LBJ 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.20 days = 30 } #LBJ-NPP transition
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1703 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Jackson"
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC #Bennett 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.18 days = 15 } #Bennett-NPP transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC #LBJ 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.20 days = 30 } #LBJ-NPP transition
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 5 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.1705 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Yockey"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 3 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.1706 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Hall"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RDC
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1741 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Goldwater"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RDC
				}
				country_event = { id = hart.misc.1 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Hart"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1744 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Smith"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1743 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Harrington"
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { #Robert McNamara
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RDC }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.a
	}
	option = { #George McGovern
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RDC }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.b
	}
	option = { #Jeane Kirkpatrick
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.c
	}
	option = { #Henry M. "Scoop" Jackson
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.d
	}
	option = { #Francis Parker Yockey
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 5 } }
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.e
	}
	option = { #Gus Hall
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 3 } }
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.f
	}
	option = { #Barry Goldwater reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RDC
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.g
	}
	option = { #John Glenn reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RDC
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.h
	}
	option = { #Margaret Chase Smith reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.i
	}
	option = { #Michael Harrington reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.j
	}
}

#Class 1
country_event = { #Show preparation and mark states for election
	id = USA_election_helpers.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_election_helpers.1" }
	title = USA_election_helpers.1.t
	desc = USA_election_helpers.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_IBR_big_meeting

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
			limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
				USA_get_nominations_for_senate = yes
				set_variable = { npp_campaign_infrastructure = 1 }
				set_variable = { rdc_campaign_infrastructure = 1 }
			}
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.2 days = 280 }
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.13 days = 100 } #Need to trigger way before the election, to show in the polls (societal unity)
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.9 days = 60 }

		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #RDs
		name = USA_election_helpers.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_senate_elections_visible_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_can_campaign_for_RD_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_class_1_senate_prepare = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_campaigning_for_RD
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes

		}
	}
	option = { #NPP
		name = USA_election_helpers.1.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_senate_elections_visible_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_can_campaign_for_NPP_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_class_1_senate_prepare = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_campaigning_for_NPP
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Actually hold the election
	id = USA_election_helpers.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_election_helpers.2" }
	title = USA_election_helpers.2.t
	desc = USA_election_helpers.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_supreme_court

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.8 days = 30 } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA_election_helpers.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_senate_elections_occur_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			# USA_hold_senate_election = yes
			USA_hold_senate_election_in_state = yes
			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_US_Election }
			remove_TNO_alert = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					date > 1972.01.01
				}
				set_variable = { senator_2_RD_D_name = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_presidential_elections
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.141 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Prep Class II election
	id = USA_election_helpers.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_election_helpers.3" }
	title = USA_election_helpers.3.t
	desc = USA_election_helpers.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_presidential_podium

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						date > 1966.01.01
						date < 1967.01.01
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_Sovereigntist_Caucus_Active
				set_country_flag = USA_Marxist_Caucus_Active
				USA_assess_NPP_unity = yes
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
				USA_get_nominations_for_senate = yes
				set_variable = { npp_campaign_infrastructure = 1 }
				set_variable = { rdc_campaign_infrastructure = 1 }
			}
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.4 days = 280 }
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.13 days = 100 } #Need to trigger way before the election, to show in the polls (societal unity)
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.9 days = 60 }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #RDs
		name = USA_election_helpers.3.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_senate_elections_visible_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_can_campaign_for_RD_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_class_2_senate_prepare = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_campaigning_for_RD
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					date > 1966.01.01
					date < 1967.01.01
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_new_caucus_tt
		}
	}
	option = { #NPP

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_can_campaign_for_NPP_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_class_2_senate_prepare = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_campaigning_for_NPP
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					date > 1966.01.01
					date < 1967.01.01
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_new_caucus_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #RD Great campaign
	id = USA.senate.1
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.senate.1"
		set_variable = { US_voting_campaign_region_prev = US_voting_campaign_region } #Purely for Tooltips
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_player_campaign_in_New_England
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = USA_campaign_region_1
					}
					add_to_variable = { rdc_campaign_infrastructure = 0.02 }
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_player_campaign_in_New_England
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_voting_campaign_region = 2 }
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = USA_campaign_region_2
					}
					add_to_variable = { rdc_campaign_infrastructure = 0.02 }
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_player_campaign_in_East_Coast
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_voting_campaign_region = 3 }
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = USA_campaign_region_3
					}
					add_to_variable = { rdc_campaign_infrastructure = 0.005 }
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_player_campaign_in_Deep_South
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_voting_campaign_region = 4 }
				}

#						option = USA_OIL_PATH_SAU_NON_INTERVENTION
#					}
#				}
#			}

#	}
	option = { #The Saudis are our friends
		name = USA.oilcrisis.102.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = SAU
				SAU = { has_capitulated = no }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			#modifier = {
			#	factor = 0
			#	OR = {
			#		has_game_rule = {
			#			rule = USA_OIL_PATH
			#			option = USA_OIL_PATH_UAR_INTERVENTION
			#		}
			#		has_game_rule = {
			#			rule = USA_OIL_PATH
			#			option = USA_OIL_PATH_UAR_NON_INTERVENTION
			#		}
			#	}
			#}
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_oil_crisis
		set_country_flag = USA_back_saudi
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_hart_presidency
				}
			}
			USA_reload_presidential_tree = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Neo Silver Act occurs
	id = USA.neo_silver.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.neo_silver.1" }
	title = USA.neo_silver.1.t
	desc = {
		text = USA.neo_silver.1.desc
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = USA.neo_silver.1.lbj_desc
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_bennett_1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.neo_silver.1.a
		set_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = -0.9 }
		econ_inflation_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.3 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.neo_silver.1.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC
				has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RDC
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = -0.5 }
		econ_inflation_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.45 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Wallace Impeached Epilogue Pt 2.
	id = USA.epilogue.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.epilogue.5" }
	title = USA.epilogue.5.t
	desc = USA.epilogue.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_wallace_microphones_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.epilogue.5.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { date < 1968.01.01 }
				country_event = { id = USA.epilogue.6 days = 730 random_days = 30 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { date < 1972.01.01 }
				country_event = { id = USA.epilogue.7 days = 730 random_days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = USA_debug.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_debug.1" }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA_debug.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_homefront_effects }
			}
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = USA_homefront_effects
			}	
		}
	}
}

	id = USA_debug.2

		add_to_variable = { USA_BONUS_rural_dem_val = 0.03 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rural_dem_shift
	}
}
########################################################
country_event = { #animation event
	id = USA.animation.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.animation.1" }
	desc = USA.animation.1.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.animation.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { US_state_position = 51 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = USA_animation_in_progress
			US_clear_animation_vars = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = US_animation_disabled
				}
				clear_array = USA_states_icon_array
				clear_array = USA_states_x_array
				clear_array = USA_states_y_array
				for_loop_effect = {
					start = 0
					end = 51
					value = idx

					add_to_array = { USA_states_x_array = USA_states_x_array_retained_order^idx }
					add_to_array = { USA_states_y_array = USA_states_y_array_retained_order^idx }
				}
				for_loop_effect = {
					start = 0
					end = 53
					value = idx

					set_variable = { USA_number_to_add = idx }
					add_to_array = { USA_states_icon_array = USA_number_to_add } 
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_no_of_presidential_elections = 1 }
			set_variable = { RDC_electoral_votes_this_election = US_voting_rdc_electoral_college_votes }
			set_variable = { NPP_electoral_votes_this_election = US_voting_npp_electoral_college_votes }
			USA_save_presidential_election_results = yes
			USA_display_election_results = yes
			##This Next Bit Will Fire The Event Which Tells You Who Won Once The Animation Is Played#
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_no_of_presidential_elections_held = 1 }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.135 } #64 Election
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_no_of_presidential_elections_held = 2 }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA_elec_prim.5 } #68 Election
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_no_of_presidential_elections_held = 3 }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA_elec_prim.15 } #72 Election
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { US_state_position = 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { US_state_position = 1 }
			USA = {
				country_event = { id = USA.animation.1 hours = 2 } #Gives time for the last animation to play
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { US_state_position < 50 }
			}
			US_animation_progress = yes
		}
	}
}
